I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Two way binding to a property of an object in an array update is delayed
### Describe the bug

If I use a complex two way binding to read and update a value on an object in an array that is inside a class _(see minimal reproduction code below)_ I get weird behaviour where the update doesn't happen until a second input. 

```html
<script>
	class MyStore {
		arrayOfComplexObjects = $state([{ value: "value" }])
		
		updateObject = (x) => {
			this.arrayOfComplexObjects = this.arrayOfComplexObjects.map(_ => ({ value:x }))
		}
	}
	
	const myStore = new MyStore();
</script>

{#each myStore.arrayOfComplexObjects as obj}
	<div>
		{obj.value}
	</div>
	<input bind:value={() => obj.value, (x) => myStore.updateObject(x)} />
{/each}

```

This issue does not occur on version 5.35.1.

### Reproduction

The issue is reproduced in a minimal reproduction here

https://svelte.dev/playground/ac953fd28f2941ef8a8f105461d061f3?version=5.38.1

### Logs

No relevant logs.

2025-12-27 00:08:49,931 - DEBUG - swea-tools-sveltejs__svelte-16649 - Retrieved state from environment: {'working_dir': '/testbed'}
2025-12-27 00:08:49,934 - INFO - swea-agent-sveltejs__svelte-16649 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/dom/elements/bindings/input.js:
     1	/** @import { Batch } from '../../../reactivity/batch.js' */
     2	import { DEV } from 'esm-env';
     3	import { render_effect, teardown } from '../../../reactivity/effects.js';
     4	import { listen_to_event_and_reset_event } from './shared.js';
     5	import * as e from '../../../errors.js';
     6	import { is } from '../../../proxy.js';
     7	import { queue_micro_task } from '../../task.js';
     8	import { hydrating } from '../../hydration.js';
     9	import { untrack } from '../../../runtime.js';
    10	import { is_runes } from '../../../context.js';
    11	import { current_batch, previous_batch } from '../../../reactivity/batch.js';
    12	
    13	/**
    14	 * @param {HTMLInputElement} input
    15	 * @param {() => unknown} get
    16	 * @param {(value: unknown) => void} set
    17	 * @returns {void}
    18	 */
    19	export function bind_value(input, get, set = get) {
    20	        var runes = is_runes();
    21	
    22	        var batches = new WeakSet();
    23	
    24	        listen_to_event_and_reset_event(input, 'input', (is_reset) => {
    25	                if (DEV && input.type === 'checkbox') {
    26	                        // TODO should this happen in prod too?
    27	                        e.bind_invalid_checkbox_value();
    28	                }
    29	
    30	                /** @type {any} */
    31	                var value = is_reset ? input.defaultValue : input.value;
    32	                value = is_numberlike_input(input) ? to_number(value) : value;
    33	                set(value);
    34	
    35	                if (current_batch !== null) {
    36	                        batches.add(current_batch);
    37	                }
    38	
    39	                // In runes mode, respect any validation in accessors (doesn't apply in legacy mode,
    40	                // because we use mutable state which ensures the render effect always runs)
    41	                if (runes && value !== (value = get())) {
    42	                        var start = input.selectionStart;
    43	                        var end = input.selectionEnd;
    44	
    45	                        // the value is coerced on assignment
    46	                        input.value = value ?? '';
    47	
    48	                        // Restore selection
    49	                        if (end !== null) {
    50	                                input.selectionStart = start;
    51	                                input.selectionEnd = Math.min(end, input.value.length);
    52	                        }
    53	                }
    54	        });
    55	
    56	        if (
    57	                // If we are hydrating and the value has since changed,
    58	                // then use the updated value from the input instead.
    59	                (hydrating && input.defaultValue !== input.value) ||
    60	                // If defaultValue is set, then value == defaultValue
    61	                // TODO Svelte 6: remove input.value check and set to empty string?
    62	                (untrack(get) == null && input.value)
    63	        ) {
    64	                set(is_numberlike_input(input) ? to_number(input.value) : input.value);
    65	
    66	                if (current_batch !== null) {
    67	                        batches.add(current_batch);
    68	                }
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        render_effect(() => {
    72	                if (DEV && input.type === 'checkbox') {
    73	                        // TODO should this happen in prod too?
    74	                        e.bind_invalid_checkbox_value();
    75	                }
    76	
    77	                var value = get();
    78	
    79	                if (input === document.activeElement) {
    80	                        // we need both, because in non-async mode, render effects run before previous_batch is set
    81	                        var batch = /** @type {Batch} */ (previous_batch ?? current_batch);
    82	
    83	                        // Never rewrite the contents of a focused input. We can get here if, for example,
    84	                        // an update is deferred because of async work depending on the input:
    85	                        //
    86	                        // <input bind:value={query}>
    87	                        // <p>{await find(query)}</p>
    88	                        if (batches.has(batch)) {
    89	                                return;
    90	                        }
    91	                }
    92	
    93	                if (is_numberlike_input(input) && value === to_number(input.value)) {
    94	                        // handles 0 vs 00 case (see https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/9959)
    95	                        return;
    96	                }
    97	
    98	                if (input.type === 'date' && !value && !input.value) {
    99	                        // Handles the case where a temporarily invalid date is set (while typing, for example with a leading 0 for the day)
   100	                        // and prevents this state from clearing the other parts of the date input (see https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/7897)
   101	                        return;
   102	                }
   103	
   104	                // don't set the value of the input if it's the same to allow
   105	                // minlength to work properly
   106	                if (value !== input.value) {
   107	                        // @ts-expect-error the value is coerced on assignment
   108	                        input.value = value ?? '';
   109	                }
   110	        });
   111	}
   112	
   113	/** @type {Set<HTMLInputElement[]>} */
   114	const pending = new Set();
   115	
   116	/**
   117	 * @param {HTMLInputElement[]} inputs
   118	 * @param {null | [number]} group_index
   119	 * @param {HTMLInputElement} input
   120	 * @param {() => unknown} get
   121	 * @param {(value: unknown) => void} set
   122	 * @returns {void}
   123	 */
   124	export function bind_group(inputs, group_index, input, get, set = get) {
   125	        var is_checkbox = input.getAttribute('type') === 'checkbox';
   126	        var binding_group = inputs;
   127	
   128	        // needs to be let or related code isn't treeshaken out if it's always false
   129	        let hydration_mismatch = false;
   130	
   131	        if (group_index !== null) {
   132	                for (var index of group_index) {
   133	                        // @ts-expect-error
   134	                        binding_group = binding_group[index] ??= [];
   135	                }
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        binding_group.push(input);
   139	
   140	        listen_to_event_and_reset_event(
   141	                input,
   142	                'change',
   143	                () => {
   144	                        // @ts-ignore
   145	                        var value = input.__value;
   146	
   147	                        if (is_checkbox) {
   148	                                value = get_binding_group_value(binding_group, value, input.checked);
   149	                        }
   150	
   151	                        set(value);
   152	                },
   153	                // TODO better default value handling
   154	                () => set(is_checkbox ? [] : null)
   155	        );
   156	
   157	        render_effect(() => {
   158	                var value = get();
   159	
   160	                // If we are hydrating and the value has since changed, then use the update value
   161	                // from the input instead.
   162	                if (hydrating && input.defaultChecked !== input.checked) {
   163	                        hydration_mismatch = true;
   164	                        return;
   165	                }
   166	
   167	                if (is_checkbox) {
   168	                        value = value || [];
   169	                        // @ts-ignore
   170	                        input.checked = value.includes(input.__value);
   171	                } else {
   172	                        // @ts-ignore
   173	                        input.checked = is(input.__value, value);
   174	                }
   175	        });
   176	
   177	        teardown(() => {
   178	                var index = binding_group.indexOf(input);
   179	
   180	                if (index !== -1) {
   181	                        binding_group.splice(index, 1);
   182	                }
   183	        });
   184	
   185	        if (!pending.has(binding_group)) {
   186	                pending.add(binding_group);
   187	
   188	                queue_micro_task(() => {
   189	                        // necessary to maintain binding group order in all insertion scenarios
   190	                        binding_group.sort((a, b) => (a.compareDocumentPosition(b) === 4 ? -1 : 1));
   191	                        pending.delete(binding_group);
   192	                });
   193	        }
   194	
   195	        queue_micro_task(() => {
   196	                if (hydration_mismatch) {
   197	                        var value;
   198	
   199	                        if (is_checkbox) {
   200	                                value = get_binding_group_value(binding_group, value, input.checked);
   201	                        } else {
   202	                                var hydration_input = binding_group.find((input) => input.checked);
   203	                                // @ts-ignore
   204	                                value = hydration_input?.__value;
   205	                        }
   206	
   207	                        set(value);
   208	                }
   209	        });
   210	}
   211	
   212	/**
   213	 * @param {HTMLInputElement} input
   214	 * @param {() => unknown} get
   215	 * @param {(value: unknown) => void} set
   216	 * @returns {void}
   217	 */
   218	export function bind_checked(input, get, set = get) {
   219	        listen_to_event_and_reset_event(input, 'change', (is_reset) => {
   220	                var value = is_reset ? input.defaultChecked : input.checked;
   221	                set(value);
   222	        });
   223	
   224	        if (
   225	                // If we are hydrating and the value has since changed,
   226	                // then use the update value from the input instead.
   227	                (hydrating && input.defaultChecked !== input.checked) ||
   228	                // If defaultChecked is set, then checked == defaultChecked
   229	                untrack(get) == null
   230	        ) {
   231	                set(input.checked);
   232	        }
   233	
   234	        render_effect(() => {
   235	                var value = get();
   236	                input.checked = Boolean(value);
   237	        });
   238	}
   239	
   240	/**
   241	 * @template V
   242	 * @param {Array<HTMLInputElement>} group
   243	 * @param {V} __value
   244	 * @param {boolean} checked
   245	 * @returns {V[]}
   246	 */
   247	function get_binding_group_value(group, __value, checked) {
   248	        /** @type {Set<V>} */
   249	        var value = new Set();
   250	
   251	        for (var i = 0; i < group.length; i += 1) {
   252	                if (group[i].checked) {
   253	                        // @ts-ignore
   254	                        value.add(group[i].__value);
   255	                }
   256	        }
   257	
   258	        if (!checked) {
   259	                value.delete(__value);
   260	        }
   261	
   262	        return Array.from(value);
   263	}
   264	
   265	/**
   266	 * @param {HTMLInputElement} input
   267	 */
   268	function is_numberlike_input(input) {
   269	        var type = input.type;
   270	        return type === 'number' || type === 'range';
   271	}
   272	
   273	/**
   274	 * @param {string} value
   275	 */
   276	function to_number(value) {
   277	        return value === '' ? null : +value;
   278	}
   279	
   280	/**
   281	 * @param {HTMLInputElement} input
   282	 * @param {() => FileList | null} get
   283	 * @param {(value: FileList | null) => void} set
   284	 */
   285	export function bind_files(input, get, set = get) {
   286	        listen_to_event_and_reset_event(input, 'change', () => {
   287	                set(input.files);
   288	        });
   289	
   290	        if (
   291	                // If we are hydrating and the value has since changed,
   292	                // then use the updated value from the input instead.
   293	                hydrating &&
   294	                input.files
   295	        ) {
   296	                set(input.files);
   297	        }
   298	
   299	        render_effect(() => {
   300	                input.files = get();
   301	        });
   302	}
   303

    12	import { is_event_attribute, is_text_attribute } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
    13	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
    14	import { is_custom_element_node } from '../../../nodes.js';
    15	import { clean_nodes, determine_namespace_for_children } from '../../utils.js';
    16	import { build_getter } from '../utils.js';
    17	import {
    18	        get_attribute_name,
    19	        build_attribute_value,
    20	        build_attribute_effect,
    21	        build_set_class,
    22	        build_set_style
    23	} from './shared/element.js';
    24	import { process_children } from './shared/fragment.js';
    25	import { build_render_statement, build_template_chunk, Memoizer } from './shared/utils.js';
    26	import { visit_event_attribute } from './shared/events.js';
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * @param {AST.RegularElement} node
    30	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    31	 */
    32	export function RegularElement(node, context) {
    33	        context.state.template.push_element(node.name, node.start);
    34	
    35	        if (node.name === 'noscript') {
    36	                context.state.template.pop_element();
    37	                return;
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        const is_custom_element = is_custom_element_node(node);
    41	
    42	        // cloneNode is faster, but it does not instantiate the underlying class of the
    43	        // custom element until the template is connected to the dom, which would
    44	        // cause problems when setting properties on the custom element.
    45	        // Therefore we need to use importNode instead, which doesn't have this caveat.
    46	        // Additionally, Webkit browsers need importNode for video elements for autoplay
    47	        // to work correctly.
    48	        context.state.template.needs_import_node ||= node.name === 'video' || is_custom_element;
    49	
    50	        context.state.template.contains_script_tag ||= node.name === 'script';
    51	
    52	        /** @type {Array<AST.Attribute | AST.SpreadAttribute>} */
    53	        const attributes = [];
    54	
    55	        /** @type {AST.ClassDirective[]} */
    56	        const class_directives = [];
    57	
    58	        /** @type {AST.StyleDirective[]} */
    59	        const style_directives = [];
    60	
    61	        /** @type {Array<AST.AnimateDirective | AST.BindDirective | AST.OnDirective | AST.TransitionDirective | AST.UseDirective | AST.AttachTag>} */
    62	        const other_directives = [];
    63	
    64	        /** @type {ExpressionStatement[]} */
    65	        const lets = [];
    66	
    67	        /** @type {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} */
    68	        const lookup = new Map();
    69	
    70	        /** @type {Map<string, AST.BindDirective>} */
    71	        const bindings = new Map();
    72	
    73	        let has_spread = node.metadata.has_spread;
    74	        let has_use = false;
    75	
    76	        for (const attribute of node.attributes) {
    77	                switch (attribute.type) {
    78	                        case 'AnimateDirective':
    79	                                other_directives.push(attribute);
    80	                                break;
    81	
    82	                        case 'Attribute':
    83	                                // `is` attributes need to be part of the template, otherwise they break
    84	                                if (attribute.name === 'is' && context.state.metadata.namespace === 'html') {
    85	                                        const { value } = build_attribute_value(attribute.value, context);
    86	
    87	                                        if (value.type === 'Literal' && typeof value.value === 'string') {
    88	                                                context.state.template.set_prop('is', value.value);
    89	                                                continue;
    90	                                        }
    91	                                }
    92	
    93	                                attributes.push(attribute);
    94	                                lookup.set(attribute.name, attribute);
    95	                                break;
    96	
    97	                        case 'BindDirective':
    98	                                bindings.set(attribute.name, attribute);
    99	                                other_directives.push(attribute);
   100	                                break;

   234	                                }
   235	
   236	                                if (name !== 'class' || value) {
   237	                                        context.state.template.set_prop(
   238	                                                attribute.name,
   239	                                                is_boolean_attribute(name) && value === true ? undefined : value === true ? '' : value
   240	                                        );
   241	                                }
   242	                        } else if (name === 'autofocus') {
   243	                                let { value } = build_attribute_value(attribute.value, context);
   244	                                context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.autofocus', node_id, value)));
   245	                        } else if (name === 'class') {
   246	                                const is_html = context.state.metadata.namespace === 'html' && node.name !== 'svg';
   247	                                build_set_class(node, node_id, attribute, class_directives, context, is_html);
   248	                        } else if (name === 'style') {
   249	                                build_set_style(node_id, attribute, style_directives, context);
   250	                        } else if (is_custom_element) {
   251	                                build_custom_element_attribute_update_assignment(node_id, attribute, context);
   252	                        } else {
   253	                                const { value, has_state } = build_attribute_value(
   254	                                        attribute.value,
   255	                                        context,
   256	                                        (value, metadata) =>
   257	                                                metadata.has_call || metadata.has_await
   258	                                                        ? context.state.memoizer.add(value, metadata.has_await)
   259	                                                        : value
   260	                                );
   261	
   262	                                const update = build_element_attribute_update(node, node_id, name, value, attributes);
   263	
   264	                                (has_state ? context.state.update : context.state.init).push(b.stmt(update));
   265	                        }
   266	                }
   267	        }
   268	
   269	        if (
   270	                is_load_error_element(node.name) &&
   271	                (has_spread || has_use || lookup.has('onload') || lookup.has('onerror'))
   272	        ) {
   273	                context.state.after_update.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.replay_events', node_id)));
   274	        }
   275	
   276	        const metadata = {
   277	                ...context.state.metadata,
   278	                namespace: determine_namespace_for_children(node, context.state.metadata.namespace)
   279	        };
   280	
   281	        if (bindings.has('innerHTML') || bindings.has('innerText') || bindings.has('textContent')) {
   282	                const contenteditable = lookup.get('contenteditable');
   283	
   284	                if (
   285	                        contenteditable &&
   286	                        (contenteditable.value === true ||
   287	                                (is_text_attribute(contenteditable) && contenteditable.value[0].data === 'true'))
   288	                ) {
   289	                        metadata.bound_contenteditable = true;
   290	                }
   291	        }
   292	
   293	        /** @type {ComponentClientTransformState} */
   294	        const state = {
   295	                ...context.state,
   296	                metadata,
   297	                scope: /** @type {Scope} */ (context.state.scopes.get(node.fragment)),
   298	                preserve_whitespace:
   299	                        context.state.preserve_whitespace || node.name === 'pre' || node.name === 'textarea'
   300	        };

    11	/**
    12	 * @param {AST.BindDirective} node
    13	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    14	 */
    15	export function BindDirective(node, context) {
    16	        const expression = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(node.expression));
    17	        const property = binding_properties[node.name];
    18	
    19	        const parent = /** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (context.path.at(-1));
    20	
    21	        let get, set;
    22	
    23	        if (expression.type === 'SequenceExpression') {
    24	                [get, set] = expression.expressions;
    25	        } else {
    26	                if (
    27	                        dev &&
    28	                        context.state.analysis.runes &&
    29	                        expression.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    30	                        (node.name !== 'this' ||

    33	                                                type === 'IfBlock' ||
    34	                                                type === 'EachBlock' ||

    40	                        validate_binding(context.state, node, expression);
    41	                }

    44	
    45	                /** @type {Expression | undefined} */
    46	                set = b.unthunk(

   193	
   194	                        case 'focused':
   195	                                call = b.call(`$.bind_focused`, context.state.node, set ?? get);
   196	                                break;
   197	
   198	                        case 'group': {
   199	                                const indexes = node.metadata.parent_each_blocks.map((each) => {
   200	                                        // if we have a keyed block with an index, the index is wrapped in a source
   201	                                        return each.metadata.keyed && each.index

   204	                                });

   206	                                // We need to additionally invoke the value attribute signal to register it as a dependency,
   207	                                // so that when the value is updated, the group binding is updated

   209

   247	        // bind:this is a special case as it's one-way and could influence the render effect.

	const defer =
		node.name !== 'this' &&
		parent.type === 'RegularElement' &&
		parent.attributes.find((a) => a.type === 'UseDirective');

	let statement = defer ? b.stmt(b.call('$.effect', b.thunk(call))) : b.stmt(call);

	// TODO this doesn't account for function bindings
	if (node.metadata.binding?.blocker) {
		statement = b.stmt(
			b.call(b.member(node.metadata.binding.blocker, b.id('then')), b.thunk(b.block([statement])))
		);
	}

	// Bindings need to happen after attribute updates, therefore after the render effect, and in order with events/actions.
	// bind:this is a special case as it's one-way and could influence the render effect.
	if (node.name === 'this') {
		context.state.init.push(statement);
	} else {
		if (defer) {
			context.state.init.push(statement);
		} else {
			context.state.after_update.push(statement);
		}
	}
}

Great! Now I can see what the issue is. The logic checks if the input is active and if the batch is the one that caused the update. But this logic uses `previous_batch ?? current_batch`, and the issue is likely that when we use functional two-way binding (with getter/setter), the batch tracking might not be working correctly.

Let me create a test to reproduce the issue:

    19	export function bind_value(input, get, set = get) {
    20	        var runes = is_runes();
    21	
    22	        var batches = new WeakSet();
    23	
    24	        listen_to_event_and_reset_event(input, 'input', (is_reset) => {
    25	                if (DEV && input.type === 'checkbox') {
    26	                        // TODO should this happen in prod too?
    27	                        e.bind_invalid_checkbox_value();
    28	                }
    29	
    30	                /** @type {any} */
    31	                var value = is_reset ? input.defaultValue : input.value;
    32	                value = is_numberlike_input(input) ? to_number(value) : value;
    33	                set(value);
    34	
    35	                if (current_batch !== null) {
    36	                        batches.add(current_batch);
    37	                }
    38	
    39	                // In runes mode, respect any validation in accessors (doesn't apply in legacy mode,
    40	                // because we use mutable state which ensures the render effect always runs)
    41	                if (runes && value !== (value = get())) {
    42	                        var start = input.selectionStart;
    43	                        var end = input.selectionEnd;
    44	
    45	                        // the value is coerced on assignment
    46	                        input.value = value ?? '';
    47	
    48	                        // Restore selection
    49	                        if (end !== null) {
    50	                                input.selectionStart = start;
    51	                                input.selectionEnd = Math.min(end, input.value.length);
    52	                        }
    53	                }
    54	        });
    55	
    56	        if (
    57	                // If we are hydrating and the value has since changed,
    58	                // then use the updated value from the input instead.
    59	                (hydrating && input.defaultValue !== input.value) ||
    60	                // If defaultValue is set, then value == defaultValue
    61	                // TODO Svelte 6: remove input.value check and set to empty string?
    62	                (untrack(get) == null && input.value)
    63	        ) {
    64	                set(is_numberlike_input(input) ? to_number(input.value) : input.value);
    65	
    66	                if (current_batch !== null) {
    67	                        batches.add(current_batch);
    68	                }
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        render_effect(() => {
    72	                if (DEV && input.type === 'checkbox') {
    73	                        // TODO should this happen in prod too?
    74	                        e.bind_invalid_checkbox_value();
    75	                }
    76	
    77	                var value = get();
    78	
    79	                if (input === document.activeElement) {
    80	                        // we need both, because in non-async mode, render effects run before previous_batch is set
    81	                        var batch = /** @type {Batch} */ (previous_batch ?? current_batch);
    82	
    83	                        // Never rewrite the contents of a focused input. We can get here if, for example,
    84	                        // an update is deferred because of async work depending on the input:
    85	                        //
    86	                        // <input bind:value={query}>
    87	                        // <p>{await find(query)}</p>
    88	                        if (batches.has(batch)) {
    89	                                return;
    90	                        }
    91	                }
    92	
    93	                if (is_numberlike_input(input) && value === to_number(input.value)) {
    94	                        // handles 0 vs 00 case (see https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/9959)
    95	                        return;
    96	                }
    97	
    98	                if (input.type === 'date' && !value && !input.value) {
    99	                        // Handles the case where a temporarily invalid date is set (while typing, for example with a leading 0 for the day)
   100	                        // and prevents this state from clearing the other parts of the date input (see https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/7897)
   101	                        return;
   102	                }
   103	
   104	                // don't set the value of the input if it's the same to allow
   105	                // minlength to work properly
   106	                if (value !== input.value) {
   107	                        // @ts-expect-error the value is coerced on assignment
   108	                        input.value = value ?? '';
   109	                }
   110	        });

Empty text block

Now I understand the issue! When the user types in the input:
1. The `input` event fires
2. Line 33: `set(value)` is called with the new value
3. Line 35-37: The current_batch is added to `batches` WeakSet
4. The `set` function (which was passed to bind_value) updates the state, triggering updates
5. The render_effect (line 71) runs
6. Line 79-90: It checks if the input is active and if the current batch is in the `batches` WeakSet. If yes, it returns early to avoid overwriting the user's input.

The problem is that when using a two-way binding with getter/setter like:
```
bind:value={() => obj.value, (x) => myStore.updateObject(x)}
```

The setter function `(x) => myStore.updateObject(x)` updates the entire array by mapping it. This creates NEW objects with the same values, which means `obj` becomes a different object reference. However, the render effect might be running in a DIFFERENT batch because the setter triggers additional state changes.

Let me check the `previous_batch` logic more closely:

    35	/** @type {Set<Batch>} */
    36	const batches = new Set();
    37	
    38	/** @type {Batch | null} */
    39	export let current_batch = null;
    40	
    41	/**
    42	 * This is needed to avoid overwriting inputs in non-async mode
    43	 * TODO 6.0 remove this, as non-async mode will go away
    44	 * @type {Batch | null}
    45	 */
    46	export let previous_batch = null;
    47	
    48	/**
    49	 * When time travelling, we re-evaluate deriveds based on the temporary
    50	 * values of their dependencies rather than their actual values, and cache
    51	 * the results in this map rather than on the deriveds themselves
    52	 * @type {Map<Derived, any> | null}
    53	 */
    54	export let batch_deriveds = null;
    55	
    56	/** @type {Set<() => void>} */
    57	export let effect_pending_updates = new Set();
    58	
    59	/** @type {Array<() => void>} */
    60	let tasks = [];
    61	
    62	function dequeue() {
    63	        const task = /** @type {() => void} */ (tasks.shift());
    64	
    65	        if (tasks.length > 0) {
    66	                queueMicrotask(dequeue);
    67	        }
    68	
    69	        task();
    70	}
    71	
    72	/** @type {Effect[]} */
    73	let queued_root_effects = [];
    74	
    75	/** @type {Effect | null} */
    76	let last_scheduled_effect = null;
    77	
    78	let is_flushing = false;
    79	
    80	let is_flushing_sync = false;
    81	export class Batch {
    82	        /**
    83	         * The current values of any sources that are updated in this batch
    84	         * They keys of this map are identical to `this.#previous`
    85	         * @type {Map<Source, any>}
    86	         */
    87	        current = new Map();
    88	
    89	        /**
    90	         * The values of any sources that are updated in this batch _before_ those updates took place.
    91	         * They keys of this map are identical to `this.#current`
    92	         * @type {Map<Source, any>}
    93	         */
    94	        #previous = new Map();
    95	
    96	        /**
    97	         * When the batch is committed (and the DOM is updated), we need to remove old branches
    98	         * and append new ones by calling the functions added inside (if/each/key/etc) blocks
    99	         * @type {Set<() => void>}
   100	         */
   101	        #callbacks = new Set();
   102	
   103	        /**
   104	         * The number of async effects that are currently in flight
   105	         */
   106	        #pending = 0;
   107	
   108	        /**
   109	         * A deferred that resolves when the batch is committed, used with `settled()`
   110	         * TODO replace with Promise.withResolvers once supported widely enough
   111	         * @type {{ promise: Promise<void>, resolve: (value?: any) => void, reject: (reason: unknown) => void } | null}
   112	         */
   113	        #deferred = null;
   114	
   115	        /**
   116	         * True if an async effect inside this batch resolved and
   117	         * its parent branch was already deleted
   118	         */
   119	        #neutered = false;
   120	
   121	        /**
   122	         * Async effects (created inside `async_derived`) encountered during processing.
   123	         * These run after the rest of the batch has updated, since they should
   124	         * always have the latest values
   125	         * @type {Effect[]}
   126	         */
   127	        #async_effects = [];
   128	
   129	        /**
   130	         * The same as `#async_effects`, but for effects inside a newly-created
   131	         * `<svelte:boundary>` — these do not prevent the batch from committing
   132	         * @type {Effect[]}
   133	         */
   134	        #boundary_async_effects = [];
   135	
   136	        /**
   137	         * Template effects and `$effect.pre` effects, which run when
   138	         * a batch is committed
   139	         * @type {Effect[]}
   140	         */
   141	        #render_effects = [];
   142	
   143	        /**
   144	         * The same as `#render_effects`, but for `$effect` (which runs after)
   145	         * @type {Effect[]}
   146	         */
   147	        #effects = [];
   148	
   149	        /**
   150	         * Block effects, which may need to re-run on subsequent flushes
   151	         * in order to update internal sources (e.g. each block items)
   152	         * @type {Effect[]}
   153	         */
   154	        #block_effects = [];
   155	
   156	        /**
   157	         * Deferred effects (which run after async work has completed) that are DIRTY
   158	         * @type {Effect[]}
   159	         */
   160	        #dirty_effects = [];
   161	
   162	        /**
   163	         * Deferred effects that are MAYBE_DIRTY
   164	         * @type {Effect[]}
   165	         */
   166	        #maybe_dirty_effects = [];
   167	
   168	        /**
   169	         * A set of branches that still exist, but will be destroyed when this batch
   170	         * is committed — we skip over these during `process`
   171	         * @type {Set<Effect>}
   172	         */
   173	        skipped_effects = new Set();
   174	
   175	        /**
   176	         *
   177	         * @param {Effect[]} root_effects
   178	         */
   179	        process(root_effects) {
   180	                queued_root_effects = [];
   181	
   182	                previous_batch = null;
   183	
   184	                /** @type {Map<Source, { v: unknown, wv: number }> | null} */
   185	                var current_values = null;
   186	
   187	                // if there are multiple batches, we are 'time travelling' —
   188	                // we need to undo the changes belonging to any batch
   189	                // other than the current one
   190	                if (batches.size > 1) {
   191	                        current_values = new Map();
   192	                        batch_deriveds = new Map();
   193	
   194	                        for (const [source, current] of this.current) {
   195	                                current_values.set(source, { v: source.v, wv: source.wv });
   196	                                source.v = current;
   197	                        }
   198	
   199	                        for (const batch of batches) {
   200	                                if (batch === this) continue;
   201	
   202	                                for (const [source, previous] of batch.#previous) {
   203	                                        if (!current_values.has(source)) {
   204	                                                current_values.set(source, { v: source.v, wv: source.wv });
   205	                                                source.v = previous;
   206	                                        }
   207	                                }
   208	                        }
   209	                }
   210	
   211	                for (const root of root_effects) {
   212	                        this.#traverse_effect_tree(root);
   213	                }
   214	
   215	                // if we didn't start any new async work, and no async work
   216	                // is outstanding from a previous flush, commit
   217	                if (this.#async_effects.length === 0 && this.#pending === 0) {
   218	                        this.#commit();
   219	
   220	                        var render_effects = this.#render_effects;
   221	                        var effects = this.#effects;
   222	
   223	                        this.#render_effects = [];
   224	                        this.#effects = [];
   225	                        this.#block_effects = [];
   226	
   227	                        // If sources are written to, then work needs to happen in a separate batch, else prior sources would be mixed with
   228	                        // newly updated sources, which could lead to infinite loops when effects run over and over again.
   229	                        previous_batch = current_batch;
   230	                        current_batch = null;
   231	
   232	                        flush_queued_effects(render_effects);
   233	                        flush_queued_effects(effects);
   234	
   235	                        // Reinstate the current batch if there was no new one created, as `process()` runs in a loop in `flush_effects()`.
   236	                        // That method expects `current_batch` to be set, and could run the loop again if effects result in new effects
   237	                        // being scheduled but without writes happening in which case no new batch is created.
   238	                        if (current_batch === null) {
   239	                                current_batch = this;
   240	                        } else {
   241	                                batches.delete(this);
   242	                        }
   243	
   244	                        this.#deferred?.resolve();
   245	                } else {
   246	                        this.#defer_effects(this.#render_effects);
   247	                        this.#defer_effects(this.#effects);
   248	                        this.#defer_effects(this.#block_effects);
   249	                }
   250	
   251	                if (current_values) {
   252	                        for (const [source, { v, wv }] of current_values) {
   253	                                // reset the source to the current value (unless
   254	                                // it got a newer value as a result of effects running)
   255	                                if (source.wv <= wv) {
   256	                                        source.v = v;
   257	                                }
   258	                        }
   259	
   260	                        batch_deriveds = null;
   261	                }
   262	
   263	                for (const effect of this.#async_effects) {
   264	                        update_effect(effect);
   265	                }
   266	
   267	                for (const effect of this.#boundary_async_effects) {
   268	                        update_effect(effect);
   269	                }
   270	
   271	                this.#async_effects = [];
   272	                this.#boundary_async_effects = [];
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        /**
   276	         * Traverse the effect tree, executing effects or stashing
   277	         * them for later execution as appropriate
   278	         * @param {Effect} root
   279	         */
   280	        #traverse_effect_tree(root) {
   281	                root.f ^= CLEAN;
   282	
   283	                var effect = root.first;
   284	
   285	                while (effect !== null) {
   286	                        var flags = effect.f;
   287	                        var is_branch = (flags & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) !== 0;
   288	                        var is_skippable_branch = is_branch && (flags & CLEAN) !== 0;

   478	/**
   479	 * Synchronously flush any pending updates.
   480	 * Returns void if no callback is provided, otherwise returns the result of calling the callback.
   481	 * @template [T=void]
   482	 * @param {(() => T) | undefined} [fn]
   483	 * @returns {T}
   484	 */
   485	export function flushSync(fn) {
   486	        if (async_mode_flag && active_effect !== null) {
   487	                e.flush_sync_in_effect();
   488	        }
   489	
   490	        var was_flushing_sync = is_flushing_sync;
   491	        is_flushing_sync = true;
   492	
   493	        try {
   494	                var result;
   495	
   496	                if (fn) {
   497	                        flush_effects();
   498	                        result = fn();
   499	                }
   500	
   501	                while (true) {
   502	                        flush_tasks();

   504	                        if (queued_root_effects.length === 0) {
   505	                                current_batch?.flush();

   507	                                // we need to check again, in case we just updated an `$effect.pending()`
   508	                                if (queued_root_effects.length === 0) {
   509	                                        // this would be reset in `flush_effects()` but since we are early returning here,
   510	                                        // we need to reset it here as well in case the first time there's 0 queued root effects
   511	                                        last_scheduled_effect = null;
   512	
   513	                                        return /** @type {T} */ (result);
   514	                                }
   515	                        }
   516	
   517	                        flush_effects();
   518	                }
   519	        } finally {
   520	                is_flushing_sync = was_flushing_sync;
   521	        }
   522	}
   523	
   524	function flush_effects() {
   525	        var was_updating_effect = is_updating_effect;
   526	        is_flushing = true;
   527	
   528	        try {
   529	                var flush_count = 0;
   530	                set_is_updating_effect(true);
   531	
   532	                while (queued_root_effects.length > 0) {
   533	                        var batch = Batch.ensure();
   534	
   535	                        if (flush_count++ > 1000) {
   536	                                if (DEV) {
   537	                                        var updates = new Map();
   538	
   539	                                        for (const source of batch.current.keys()) {
   540	                                                for (const [stack, update] of source.updated ?? []) {
   541	                                                        var entry = updates.get(stack);
   542	
   543	                                                        if (!entry) {
   544	                                                                entry = { error: update.error, count: 0 };
   545	                                                                updates.set(stack, entry);
   546	                                                        }
   547	
   548	                                                        entry.count += update.count;
   549	                                                }
   550	                                        }
   551	
   552	                                        for (const update of updates.values()) {
   553	                                                // eslint-disable-next-line no-console
   554	                                                console.error(update.error);
   555	                                        }
   556	                                }
   557	
   558	                                infinite_loop_guard();
   559	                        }
   560	
   561	                        batch.process(queued_root_effects);
   562	                        old_values.clear();
   563	                }
   564	        } finally {
   565	                is_flushing = false;
   566	                set_is_updating_effect(was_updating_effect);
   567	
   568	                last_scheduled_effect = null;
   569	        }
   570	}
   571	
   572	function infinite_loop_guard() {
   573	        try {
   574	                e.effect_update_depth_exceeded();
   575	        } catch (error) {
   576	                if (DEV) {
   577	                        // stack contains no useful information, replace it
   578	                        define_property(error, 'stack', { value: '' });
   579	                }
   580	
   581	                // Best effort: invoke the boundary nearest the most recent
   582	                // effect and hope that it's relevant to the infinite loop
   583	                invoke_error_boundary(error, last_scheduled_effect);
   584	        }
   585	}

   587	/** @type {Effect[] | null} */
   588	export let eager_block_effects = null;
   589	
   590	/**
   591	 * @param {Array<Effect>} effects
   592	 * @returns {void}
   593	 */
   594	function flush_queued_effects(effects) {
   595	        var length = effects.length;
   596	        if (length === 0) return;
   597	
   598	        var i = 0;
   599	
   600	        while (i < length) {
   601	                var effect = effects[i++];
   602	
   603	                if ((effect.f & (DESTROYED | INERT)) === 0 && is_dirty(effect)) {
   604	                        eager_block_effects = [];
   605	
   606	                        update_effect(effect);
   607	
   608	                        // Effects with no dependencies or teardown do not get added to the effect tree.
   609	                        // Deferred effects (e.g. `$effect(...)`) _are_ added to the tree because we
   610	                        // don't know if we need to keep them until they are executed. Doing the check
   611	                        // here (rather than in `update_effect`) allows us to skip the work for
   612	                        // immediate effects.
   613	                        if (effect.deps === null && effect.first === null && effect.nodes_start === null) {
   614	                                // if there's no teardown or abort controller we completely unlink
   615	                                // the effect from the graph
   616	                                if (effect.teardown === null && effect.ac === null) {
   617	                                        // remove this effect from the graph
   618	                                        unlink_effect(effect);
   619	                                } else {
   620	                                        // keep the effect in the graph, but free up some memory
   621	                                        effect.fn = null;
   622	                                }
   623	                        }
   624	
   625	                        if (eager_block_effects.length > 0) {
   626	                                // TODO this feels incorrect! it gets the tests passing
   627	                                old_values.clear();
   628	
   629	                                for (const e of eager_block_effects) {
   630	                                        update_effect(e);
   631	                                }
   632	
   633	                                eager_block_effects = [];
   634	                        }
   635	                }
   636	        }
   637	
   638	        eager_block_effects = null;
   639	}
   640	
   641	/**
   642	 * @param {Effect} signal
   643	 * @returns {void}
   644	 */
   645	export function schedule_effect(signal) {
   646	        var effect = (last_scheduled_effect = signal);
   647	
   648	        while (effect.parent !== null) {
   649	                effect = effect.parent;
   650	                var flags = effect.f;
   651	
   652	                // if the effect is being scheduled because a parent (each/await/etc) block
   653	                // updated an internal source, bail out or we'll cause a second flush
   654	                if (is_flushing && effect === active_effect && (flags & BLOCK_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   655	                        return;
   656	                }
   657	
   658	                if ((flags & (ROOT_EFFECT | BRANCH_EFFECT)) !== 0) {
   659	                        if ((flags & CLEAN) === 0) return;
   660	                        effect.f ^= CLEAN;
   661	                }
   662	        }
   663	
   664	        queued_root_effects.push(effect);
   665	}

Now I can see the issue more clearly. Look at line 229 of batch.js:
```javascript
previous_batch = current_batch;
current_batch = null;
```

The `previous_batch` is set when committing a batch. The logic in bind_value (line 81 of input.js) is:
```javascript
var batch = /** @type {Batch} */ (previous_batch ?? current_batch);
```

The issue is that when the setter function in a two-way binding triggers state updates, a new batch might be created. If that happens, `current_batch` becomes the new batch, and when the render_effect runs, it will look for either `previous_batch` or `current_batch`. But the `batches` WeakSet only contains the original batch (the one where the input event occurred).

Let me trace through what happens:

1. User types "a" → input event fires
2. `set(value)` is called where `set = (x) => myStore.updateObject(x)`
3. `current_batch` is added to the `batches` WeakSet (let's call it Batch1)
4. The setter function `myStore.updateObject(x)` executes:
   - It maps the array, creating NEW objects
   - This creates state changes which might create a NEW batch (Batch2) 
5. The render_effect runs:
   - It tries to get the value with `get()` which returns `obj.value`
   - But `obj` is now a different object (from the map operation)!
   - It checks `previous_batch ?? current_batch` (which could be Batch2)
   - Batch2 is NOT in the `batches` WeakSet (only Batch1 is)
   - So it doesn't return early, and overwrites the input value with "value" (the old value)

The fix should be to ensure that when we call `set(value)` in the input event handler, we track ALL batches that get created as a result of that setter, not just the current one.

Let me check if there's a way to do this. Looking at the code, I need to understand when `previous_batch` is set and cleared:

So `previous_batch` is:

- Set to `current_batch` at line 229 (after committing and before flushing effects)

Looking at this more carefully, I think the real issue is that when we use a getter/setter binding, the `get()` function might be reading from a different object after the `set()` function has updated the state. This is exactly what happens in the reproduction case - the array is mapped, creating new objects.

Let me think about the fix:

**Option 1**: Track the batch at the time of calling `set()`, and also track any batches that are created/activated during the execution of `set()`. This is complex.

**Option 2**: After calling `set(value)`, immediately call `get()` and check if the value matches. If it doesn't, we should still add the batch to the WeakSet. This way, even if the getter returns a different value due to object recreation, we still know that the change originated from this input.

    // the value is coerced on assignment

    // Restore selection

 * @param {HTMLElement} element
 * @param {string} event
 * @param {(is_reset?: true) => void} handler
 * @param {(is_reset?: true) => void} [on_reset]
 */
export function listen_to_event_and_reset_event(element, event, handler, on_reset = handler) {
	element.addEventListener(event, () => without_reactive_context(handler));
	// @ts-expect-error
	const prev = element.__on_r;
	if (prev) {
		// special case for checkbox that can have multiple binds (group & checked)
		// @ts-expect-error
		element.__on_r = () => {
			prev();
			on_reset(true);
		};

Good, so the event handler runs without a reactive context. Now let me trace what happens when `set()` is called:

1. `set(value)` is called
2. This triggers the setter function created in BindDirective.js
3. The setter function is: `($$value) => { assignment to node.expression }`
4. This assignment might trigger reactive updates
5. A batch is created/ensured
6. After `set()` returns, we capture the current_batch

So when we have a complex two-way binding like:
```html
<input bind:value={() => obj.value, (x) => myStore.updateObject(x)} />
```

The `set` function is `(x) => myStore.updateObject(x)`, not an assignment expression. So it's just a plain function call that doesn't go through the AssignmentExpression visitor.

Now, when `myStore.updateObject(x)` runs, it does:
```javascript
this.arrayOfComplexObjects = this.arrayOfComplexObjects.map(_ => ({ value:x }))
```

This IS an assignment to a reactive `$state()` property, which will:
1. Trigger setters on the proxy
2. Create/ensure a batch
3. Schedule effects

But the effects won't run until the batch is flushed, which happens asynchronously (unless we're in a flushSync).

So the sequence is:
1. Input event handler runs
2. `set(value)` is called → `myStore.updateObject(value)` executes
3. Assignment to `arrayOfComplexObjects` creates a batch (or uses existing one)
4. Effects are scheduled but not run yet
5. `set(value)` returns
6. Line 36 of input.js: `current_batch` is added to `batches` WeakSet
7. Input event handler returns
8. Batch is flushed
9. Render effects run

So the batch tracking should work correctly...

Unless! Let me check one more thing. What if `set()` is called outside of a batch context? Let me look at the batch creation logic:

   156	        let new_value = should_proxy ? proxy(value) : value;
   157	
   158	        if (DEV) {
   159	                tag_proxy(new_value, /** @type {string} */ (source.label));
   160	        }
   161	
   162	        return internal_set(source, new_value);
   163	}
   164	
   165	/**
   166	 * @template V
   167	 * @param {Source<V>} source
   168	 * @param {V} value
   169	 * @returns {V}
   170	 */
   171	export function internal_set(source, value) {
   172	        if (!source.equals(value)) {
   173	                var old_value = source.v;
   174	
   175	                if (is_destroying_effect) {
   176	                        old_values.set(source, value);
   177	                } else {
   178	                        old_values.set(source, old_value);
   179	                }
   180	
   181	                source.v = value;
   182	
   183	                var batch = Batch.ensure();
   184	                batch.capture(source, old_value);
   185	
   186	                if (DEV) {
   187	                        if (tracing_mode_flag || active_effect !== null) {
   188	                                const error = get_stack('UpdatedAt');
   189	
   190	                                if (error !== null) {
   191	                                        source.updated ??= new Map();
   192	                                        let entry = source.updated.get(error.stack);
   193	
   194	                                        if (!entry) {
   195	                                                entry = { error, count: 0 };
   196	                                                source.updated.set(error.stack, entry);
   197	                                        }
   198	
   199	                                        entry.count++;
   200	                                }

Perfect! Line 183 shows that `Batch.ensure()` is called when setting a source. This ensures that a batch exists. So when `set(value)` is called in the input event handler, `Batch.ensure()` will create or return the current batch.

Now, looking at line 36 of input.js again:
```javascript
if (current_batch !== null) {
    batches.add(current_batch);
}
```

This should add the current batch to the WeakSet. So far so good.

But wait! Let me check what happens when the render_effect runs. Let me look at when render_effects are scheduled and run:

From batch.js line 229-233:
```javascript
previous_batch = current_batch;
current_batch = null;

flush_queued_effects(render_effects);
flush_queued_effects(effects);
```

So when render_effects run:
- `previous_batch` = the batch that was just committed
- `current_batch` = null

And in input.js line 81:
```javascript
var batch = /** @type {Batch} */ (previous_batch ?? current_batch);
```

So `batch = previous_batch`.

And line 88:
```javascript
if (batches.has(batch)) {
    return;
}
```

This should work! The batch should be in the WeakSet...

Unless there's a timing issue. Let me think about when the render_effect for the binding runs relative to when the each block updates.

AH! I think I found it. The issue might be that the each block creates a NEW input element and a NEW binding when the array is updated. If the array is completely replaced (not just mutated), the each block might:
1. Remove the old DOM node (including the old input)
2. Create a new DOM node (including a new input)
3. The NEW input has a NEW binding with a NEW `batches` WeakSet

So the sequence might be:
1. User types "a" in OLD input
2. Input event fires on OLD input
3. OLD binding's `set()` is called
4. State is updated
5. `current_batch` is added to OLD binding's `batches` WeakSet
6. Batch is flushed
7. Each block realizes the array changed
8. OLD input is removed from DOM
9. NEW input is created and added to DOM
10. NEW binding is set up with empty `batches` WeakSet
11. NEW binding's render_effect runs
12. It calls `get()` which returns `obj.value`
13. But `batches.has(batch)` is false (because this is a NEW binding with empty WeakSet)
14. So it sets the input value, overwriting the user's input

But wait, if the OLD input was removed from DOM, then the user wouldn't see the change at all. Unless... the input element is reused by Svelte's reconciliation?

Let me think about this differently. In Svelte's each blocks, when the data changes, Svelte tries to reuse DOM nodes if possible. If the key is not provided or if the item identity changes, Svelte might remove and recreate nodes.

In the reproduction case:
```javascript
{#each myStore.arrayOfComplexObjects as obj}
```

There's no key specified, so Svelte uses index-based reconciliation. Since the array still has one element, Svelte might reuse the DOM node but update the bindings.

But the bindings are set up during component initialization, not during updates... or are they?

   119	export function each(node, flags, get_collection, get_key, render_fn, fallback_fn = null) {
   120	        var anchor = node;
   121	
   122	        /** @type {EachState} */
   123	        var state = { flags, items: new Map(), first: null };
   124	
   125	        var is_controlled = (flags & EACH_IS_CONTROLLED) !== 0;
   126	
   127	        if (is_controlled) {
   128	                var parent_node = /** @type {Element} */ (node);
   129	
   130	                anchor = hydrating
   131	                        ? set_hydrate_node(/** @type {Comment | Text} */ (get_first_child(parent_node)))
   132	                        : parent_node.appendChild(create_text());
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        if (hydrating) {
   136	                hydrate_next();
   137	        }
   138	
   139	        /** @type {Effect | null} */
   140	        var fallback = null;
   141	
   142	        var was_empty = false;
   143	
   144	        /** @type {Map<any, EachItem>} */
   145	        var offscreen_items = new Map();
   146	
   147	        // TODO: ideally we could use derived for runes mode but because of the ability
   148	        // to use a store which can be mutated, we can't do that here as mutating a store
   149	        // will still result in the collection array being the same from the store
   150	        var each_array = derived_safe_equal(() => {
   151	                var collection = get_collection();
   152	
   153	                return is_array(collection) ? collection : collection == null ? [] : array_from(collection);
   154	        });
   155	
   156	        /** @type {V[]} */
   157	        var array;
   158	
   159	        /** @type {Effect} */
   160	        var each_effect;
   161	
   162	        function commit() {
   163	                reconcile(
   164	                        each_effect,
   165	                        array,
   166	                        state,
   167	                        offscreen_items,
   168	                        anchor,
   169	                        render_fn,
   170	                        flags,
   171	                        get_key,
   172	                        get_collection
   173	                );
   174	
   175	                if (fallback_fn !== null) {
   176	                        if (array.length === 0) {
   177	                                if (fallback) {
   178	                                        resume_effect(fallback);
   179	                                } else {
   180	                                        fallback = branch(() => fallback_fn(anchor));
   181	                                }
   182	                        } else if (fallback !== null) {
   183	                                pause_effect(fallback, () => {
   184	                                        fallback = null;
   185	                                });
   186	                        }
   187	                }
   188	        }
   189

Good! Now let me check what flags are used in the compiled output. Let me look at the compiled code again:

```javascript
$.each(node, 17, () => items, $.index, ($$anchor, item, $$index) => {
```

The flags are `17`. Let's check what this is in binary:
- 17 = 10001 in binary
- Bit 0 (EACH_ITEM_REACTIVE = 1): SET
- Bit 1 (EACH_INDEX_REACTIVE = 2): NOT SET
- Bit 2 (EACH_IS_CONTROLLED = 4): NOT SET
- Bit 3 (EACH_IS_ANIMATED = 8): NOT SET
- Bit 4 (EACH_ITEM_IMMUTABLE = 16): SET

So the flags are EACH_ITEM_REACTIVE | EACH_ITEM_IMMUTABLE.

The `EACH_ITEM_REACTIVE` flag means that the item value is reactive and will be updated using `internal_set(item.v, value)` when the array changes.

So when the array is updated from `[{ value: "value" }]` to `[{ value: "a" }]`, the each block reconciliation will:
1. Check if the key matches (since no key is specified, it uses index)
2. The item at index 0 already exists
3. Call `update_item(item, new_value, 0, flags)`
4. Since EACH_ITEM_REACTIVE is set, it calls `internal_set(item.v, new_value)`
5. This updates the source, triggering reactivity

But this means the DOM nodes are REUSED, not recreated! So the binding should also be reused.

OK so my theory about the binding being recreated was wrong. The binding is reused. But the item value is updated using `internal_set(item.v, new_value)`.

Wait, let me re-examine the compiled code:

```javascript
$.bind_value(input, () => $.get(item).value, (x) => ($.get(item).value = x));
```

The getter is `() => $.get(item).value`. This calls `$.get(item)` which gets the current value of the `item` source.

When the array is updated from `[{ value: "value" }]` to `[{ value: "a" }]`:
1. `internal_set(item.v, { value: "a" })` is called
2. This sets the source to the new object `{ value: "a" }`
3. The binding's render_effect runs (because it depends on `item`)
4. It calls `get()` which calls `$.get(item).value`
5. `$.get(item)` returns `{ value: "a" }`
6. `.value` returns `"a"`
7. So the getter should return `"a"`, not `"value"`!

So theoretically, the getter should return the correct value... unless there's a timing issue.

Let me think about the order of operations again:

1. User types "a" in input
2. Input event fires
3. `set("a")` is called, which calls `myStore.updateObject("a")`
4. `myStore.updateObject("a")` sets `this.arrayOfComplexObjects = this.arrayOfComplexObjects.map(_ => ({ value: "a" }))`
5. This triggers reactivity, creating/ensuring a batch
6. Line 36 of input.js: `current_batch` is added to `batches` WeakSet
7. The batch is processed:
   a. Each block's effect runs, sees the new array
   b. Reconcile function updates `item.v` to the new object `{ value: "a" }`
   c. This triggers render_effects that depend on `item`
   d. The binding's render_effect runs
8. In the binding's render_effect:
   a. Line 77: `value = get()` calls `$.get(item).value`
   b. `$.get(item)` should return `{ value: "a" }`
   c. So `value` should be `"a"`
   d. Line 79-90: Check if input is active and batch is tracked
   e. Line 88: `batches.has(batch)` should be true
   f. Return early, don't overwrite input

This should work correctly! But apparently it doesn't according to the bug report.

Let me think... maybe the issue is that the render_effect for the binding runs BEFORE the each block's reconcile function has updated `item.v`?

Let me check the order of effects. The each block creates a `block()` effect, and the binding creates a `render_effect()`. Let me see which runs first:

So `block()` creates a BLOCK_EFFECT, and `render_effect()` creates a RENDER_EFFECT. Let me check the batch processing order to see which runs first:

From batch.js lines 295-307:

```javascript
} else if ((flags & EFFECT) !== 0) {
    this.#effects.push(effect);
} else if (async_mode_flag && (flags & RENDER_EFFECT) !== 0) {
    this.#render_effects.push(effect);
} else if ((flags & CLEAN) === 0) {
    if ((flags & ASYNC) !== 0) {
        var effects = effect.b?.pending ? this.#boundary_async_effects : this.#async_effects;
        effects.push(effect);
    } else if (is_dirty(effect)) {
        if ((effect.f & BLOCK_EFFECT) !== 0) this.#block_effects.push(effect);
        update_effect(effect);
    }
}
```

So BLOCK_EFFECT is updated immediately during traversal (line 305), while RENDER_EFFECT is pushed to `#render_effects` to be flushed later (line 298). And from lines 220-233:

```javascript
var render_effects = this.#render_effects;
var effects = this.#effects;

this.#render_effects = [];
this.#effects = [];
this.#block_effects = [];

// If sources are written to, then work needs to happen in a separate batch, else prior sources would be mixed with
// newly updated sources, which could lead to infinite loops when effects run over and over again.
previous_batch = current_batch;
current_batch = null;

flush_queued_effects(render_effects);
flush_queued_effects(effects);
```

So the order is:
1. BLOCK_EFFECT runs during traversal (updates `item.v`)
2. Batch commits
3. `previous_batch = current_batch` is set
4. `current_batch = null`
5. RENDER_EFFECT runs (the binding's render_effect)

So by the time the binding's render_effect runs, the `item.v` should have been updated to the new object. So `get()` should return the correct value.

Hmm, but wait. Let me re-read the compiled code for the binding:

```javascript
$.bind_value(input, () => $.get(item).value, (x) => ($.get(item).value = x));
```

Actually, looking at the reproduction case more carefully:

```javascript
<input bind:value={() => obj.value, (x) => myStore.updateObject(x)} />
```

The setter is NOT `(x) => obj.value = x`, it's `(x) => myStore.updateObject(x)`.

And `myStore.updateObject(x)` does:
```javascript
this.arrayOfComplexObjects = this.arrayOfComplexObjects.map(_ => ({ value:x }))
```

This REPLACES the array with a new array containing NEW objects!

So when the setter runs:
1. Input event fires with value "a"
2. Setter `myStore.updateObject("a")` is called
3. Array is replaced: `[old_obj]` → `[new_obj]` where `new_obj = { value: "a" }`
4. But `obj` in the getter still refers to `old_obj` which has `value: "value"`!

The key insight is that the setter doesn't update `obj.value`, it replaces the entire array with new objects. So when the getter tries to read `obj.value`, it's reading from the OLD object that's no longer in the array!

Let me verify this by checking the compiled output again:

```javascript
$.each(node, 17, () => items, $.index, ($$anchor, item, $$index) => {
    var input = root_1();

    $.remove_input_defaults(input);
    $.bind_value(input, () => $.get(item).value, (x) => ($.get(item).value = x));
    $.append($$anchor, input);
});
```

Wait, this is for a simpler case where the setter is `(x) => item.value = x`. Let me compile the actual reproduction case:

🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test2.svelte << 'EOF'
<script>
	class MyStore {
		arrayOfComplexObjects = $state([{ value: "value" }])
		
		updateObject = (x) => {
			this.arrayOfComplexObjects = this.arrayOfComplexObjects.map(_ => ({ value:x }))
		}
	}
	
	const myStore = new MyStore();
</script>

{#each myStore.arrayOfComplexObjects as obj}
	<div>
		{obj.value}
	</div>
	<input bind:value={() => obj.value, (x) => myStore.updateObject(x)} />
{/each}
EOF

The getter returns the old value "value", which doesn\'t match the input value "a", so the code "restores" the input to "value".\n\nThis validation logic is meant to handle cases where the setter coerces or validates the value (e.g., `bind:value` on a number input). 2025-12-27 00:21:08,014 - INFO - swea-agent-sveltejs__svelte-16649 - 💭 THOUGHT
Empty text block

Great! So the compiled output is:
```javascript
$.bind_value(input, () => $.get(obj).value, (x) => myStore.updateObject(x));
```

And note that `obj` is a parameter to the each block's render function. When the array is replaced with a new array containing new objects, the each block will update `obj.v` (the source) to point to the new object.

Wait, let me check this. When the array is `[{ value: "value" }]` and it's replaced with `[{ value: "a" }]`, what happens to `obj`?

`obj` is created as a Source in the each block's create_item function. When reconcile is called and the item at index 0 is updated, it calls `update_item(item, new_value, 0, flags)`, which calls `internal_set(item.v, new_value)`. So `obj.v` (the source value) is updated to the new object `{ value: "a" }`.

So when the binding's getter calls `$.get(obj).value`:
- `$.get(obj)` returns `obj.v`, which is `{ value: "a" }`
- `.value` returns `"a"`

So the getter SHOULD return the correct value! Unless... there's a timing issue or the render_effect runs before the each block's reconcile?

Let me trace through the exact sequence of events one more time, paying close attention to timing:

**Initial state:**
- `myStore.arrayOfComplexObjects = [{ value: "value" }]`
- Each block has rendered with `obj.v = { value: "value" }`
- Input shows "value"

**User types "a":**
1. Input event fires
2. Line 24-54 of input.js: Event handler runs
   - Line 31-32: `value = "a"`
   - Line 33: `set("a")` calls `myStore.updateObject("a")`
     - Inside updateObject: `this.arrayOfComplexObjects = [{ value: "a" }]` (new array, new object)
     - This triggers reactivity: `Batch.ensure()` is called
     - The each block's dependency on `arrayOfComplexObjects` is marked dirty
   - Line 35-37: `current_batch` is added to `batches` WeakSet (let's call this Batch1)
   - Line 41: `value = get()` calls `$.get(obj).value`
     - `obj.v` is still `{ value: "value" }` because the each block hasn't updated yet!
     - Returns "value"
   - Line 41: Comparison `"a" !== "value"` is true
   - Lines 42-53: Cursor restoration logic runs, sets input.value to "value"

3. Event handler returns
4. Batch is flushed
5. Each block's effect runs, calls reconcile
6. `internal_set(obj.v, { value: "a" })` is called
7. Render effects are flushed
8. Binding's render_effect runs
   - Line 77: `value = get()` returns "a" (now correct)
   - Line 79-90: Input is active, check batch
   - Line 88: `batches.has(Batch1)` is true
   - Returns early, doesn't overwrite input
9. But the input already shows "value" from step 2!

AH! There it is! The issue is in lines 41-53 of input.js. After calling `set(value)`, the code immediately calls `get()` to validate the value. But at this point, the each block hasn't updated yet, so `obj.v` still points to the old object. The getter returns the old value "value", which doesn't match the input value "a", so the code "restores" the input to "value".

This validation logic is meant to handle cases where the setter coerces or validates the value (e.g., `bind:value` on a number input). But in this case, the setter doesn't immediately update the value that the getter reads from, because it updates a different part of the state (the array), which will eventually update the each block item, which will eventually update `obj.v`.

The fix should be to either:
1. Not do the validation/restoration immediately, or
2. Track the batch even for this restoration, or
3. Be smarter about when to do the restoration

Looking at the code more carefully, the restoration happens at lines 42-53:

```javascript
// In runes mode, respect any validation in accessors (doesn't apply in legacy mode,
// because we use mutable state which ensures the render effect always runs)
if (runes && value !== (value = get())) {
    var start = input.selectionStart;
    var end = input.selectionEnd;

    // the value is coerced on assignment
    input.value = value ?? '';

    // Restore selection
    if (end !== null) {
        input.selectionStart = start;
        input.selectionEnd = Math.min(end, input.value.length);
    }
}
```

This code is trying to handle the case where the setter modifies the value (e.g., validation or coercion). But it's causing issues when the setter doesn't immediately update the value that the getter reads from.

The fix should be to NOT immediately overwrite the input value when the getter returns a different value, OR to add the batch to the WeakSet even in this case. Actually, the batch IS added to the WeakSet at lines 35-37, which happens BEFORE the validation at line 41. So that should be fine.

But wait, the issue is that the input value is overwritten at line 46, which happens SYNCHRONOUSLY during the input event handler. So the user types "a", and immediately the input is set back to "value", before they can even see it.

The solution should be to NOT immediately restore the input value when `get()` returns a different value. Instead, we should wait for the render_effect to handle it. The render_effect will check if the batch is tracked and skip the update if necessary.

So the fix is to remove the immediate validation/restoration logic at lines 41-53, or to make it conditional on whether the input is focused and the batch is tracked.

Actually, let me think about this more carefully. The validation logic is there for a good reason - to handle cases like:
```html
<input bind:value={num} type="number" />
```

Where the value might be coerced or validated by the setter.

But the issue is that this validation happens too early. The correct fix should be to NOT overwrite the input during the input event handler if the input is focused. The render_effect will handle syncing the value later, and it has the batch tracking logic to avoid overwriting user input.

So the fix is to skip the immediate validation/restoration at lines 41-53 when the input is focused. Let me implement this fix:

🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_fix.js << 'EOF'
// Simulate the issue
let batches = new WeakSet();
let runes = true;
let obj = { value: "value" };
let document = {
    activeElement: null
};

// Simulate input element
let input = {
    value: "value",
    selectionStart: 0,
    selectionEnd: 0,
    equals(other) { return this === other; }
};

document.activeElement = input;

let current_batch = {};

// Simulate the getter
function get() {
    return obj.value;
}

// Simulate the setter
function set(value) {
    // This would normally update state
    console.log(`set(${value})`);
}

// Simulate the input event handler (simplified)
function handleInput() {
    let value = input.value;
    console.log(`Input value: ${value}`);
    
    set(value);
    
    if (current_batch !== null) {
        batches.add(current_batch);
        console.log('Added batch to WeakSet');
    }
    
    // The old code (without fix):
    // if (runes && value !== (value = get())) {
    //     console.log(`Validation failed, restoring to: ${value}`);
    //     input.value = value ?? '';
    // }
    
    // The new code (with fix):
    if (runes && input !== document.activeElement && value !== (value = get())) {
        console.log(`Validation failed, restoring to: ${value}`);
        input.value = value ?? '';
    } else {
        console.log('Skipped validation because input is focused');
    }
}

// Test: User types "a"
console.log('\n=== Test 1: User types "a" ===');
input.value = "a";
handleInput();
console.log(`Final input value: ${input.value}`);

// Test: Input loses focus
console.log('\n=== Test 2: Input loses focus ===');
document.activeElement = null;
input.value = "b";
handleInput();
console.log(`Final input value: ${input.value}`);
EOF
